<script>
    $(function(){
        var coronaDiagram = setInterval(function(){
         if ($('#prop-container').hasClass('active-lt')) {
            $('#prop-container').removeClass('active-lt');
            $('#prop-container').addClass('active-world');
            $('#prop-container div').each(function(){
                $(this).css("width", $(this).attr("data-world") + "%")
            })
         } else {
            $('#prop-container').removeClass('active-world');
            $('#prop-container').addClass('active-lt');
            $('#prop-container div').each(function(){
                $(this).css("width", $(this).attr("data-lt") + "%")
            })
             
         }
         $('#covi19-block .corona-stats div .location').toggleClass('active');
         
        }, 10000);


        $("#covi19-block .corona-stats div .location").click(function(){
            if (!$(this).hasClass('active')) {

                if ($(this).hasClass('lt')) {
                    $('#prop-container').removeClass('active-world');
                    $('#prop-container').addClass('active-lt');
                    $('#prop-container div').each(function(){
                        $(this).css("width", $(this).attr("data-lt") + "%")
                    });

                    $('#covi19-block .corona-stats div .location').toggleClass('active');
                } else {
                    $('#prop-container').removeClass('active-lt');
                    $('#prop-container').addClass('active-world');
                    $('#prop-container div').each(function(){
                        $(this).css("width", $(this).attr("data-world") + "%")
                    });

                    $('#covi19-block .corona-stats div .location').toggleClass('active');
                }
                clearInterval(coronaDiagram);
            }
        });
    });

</script>

<script>
	
	$(function() {
		if (_dlf.is_user_customer){
			$('#iscustomer').val('TAIP');
		}
	});
	
	$(function() {	
		$(document).on('click', '#__asksb', function() {
			var isFormValid = true;
			isFormValid = isEmpty();
			if (isFormValid ){
					$.ajax({
						url: 'https://www.delfi.lt/plius/misc/askme.php',
						type: 'POST',
						data: new FormData($('#askme-form')[0]),
						contentType: false,       
						cache: false,             
						processData:false,  
						dataType: 'json',
							success: function(response) {
								if (response.status == '1') {
									$('#askme-form').slideUp(function() {
									$('.success-report-message').css('padding-top','15px');
									$('.success-report-message').text(response.message).slideDown();
								});
								} else {
									$('.ask-report-message').text(response.message).addClass('error').slideDown();
								}
							}
						});
				}					
			return false;
		})
	});

function isEmpty(){ 
	var isFormValid = true; 
	if($('#__mrct').val() == "")
    {
	    $('.ask-report-message').css('color', '#dd5353')
		$('.ask-report-message').text('Įveskite klausimą')
		isFormValid = false
    }
   return isFormValid;
}
</script>

	$('#video-stars-container .video-stars-content').find('a').click(function(){
		var href = $(this).attr('href');
		if ($(this).hasClass('title')){
			var title = $(this).text();
		} else {
			var img = $(this).children('img')[0];
			var title = $(img).attr('alt');
		}
		var sendEvent = href + '  |  ' + title;
		ga('send', 'event', 'VideoStars', sendEvent);
	});
